        // Unified pricing selection
        function selectPlan(plan) {
            const plans = {
                strategic: { price: 199, name: 'STRATEGIC' },
                deep: { price: 499, name: 'DEEP' }, 
                quantum: { price: 999, name: 'QUANTUM' }
            };
            
            const selected = plans[plan];
            alert(`Selected ${selected.name} plan for $${selected.price}/month. Redirecting to payment...`);
            // Here would be integration with payment system
        }
    </script>

css
/* Unified Navigation */
.nav-divider {
    width: 1px;
    height: 20px;
    background: var(--matrix-border);
    margin: 0 1rem;
}

/* Unified Pricing Matrix */
.unified-pricing {
    padding: 4rem 0;
    background: var(--matrix-bg-secondary);
}

.pricing-matrix {
    display: grid;
    grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fit, minmax(300px, 1fr));
    gap: 2rem;
    margin-top: 3rem;
}

.plan-card {
    background: white;
    border-radius: 12px;
    padding: 2rem;
    box-shadow: 0 4px 20px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
    border: 2px solid transparent;
    transition: all 0.3s ease;
}

.plan-card.featured {
    border-color: var(--matrix-accent);
    transform: scale(1.05);
}

.plan-card.strategic .plan-header h3 { color: #00b4ff; }
.plan-card.deep .plan-header h3 { color: #00dc82; }
.plan-card.quantum .plan-header h3 { color: #8b5cf6; }

.plan-header {
    text-align: center;
    margin-bottom: 1.5rem;
}

.plan-header .price {
    font-size: 2.5rem;
    font-weight: bold;
    margin: 1rem 0;
}

.plan-header .price span {
    font-size: 1rem;
    color: var(--matrix-text-secondary);
}

.plan-features {

    <script>
        // Unified pricing selection
        function selectPlan(plan) {
            const plans = {
                strategic: { price: 199, name: 'STRATEGIC' },
                deep: { price: 499, name: 'DEEP' }, 
                quantum: { price: 999, name: 'QUANTUM' }
            };
            
            const selected = plans[plan];
            alert(`Selected ${selected.name} plan for $${selected.price}/month. Redirecting to payment...`);
            // Here would be integration with payment system
        }
    </script>
</body>
</html>

        }

<script>
    // Unified pricing selection
    function selectPlan(plan) {
        const plans = {
            strategic: { price: 199, name: 'STRATEGIC' },
            deep: { price: 499, name: 'DEEP' }, 
            quantum: { price: 999, name: 'QUANTUM' }
        };
        
        const selected = plans[plan];
        alert(`Selected ${selected.name} plan for $${selected.price}/month. Redirecting to payment...`);
        // Here would be integration with payment system
    }
</script>
